It supports both objective calibration (with Dolby Tone) and subjective estimation (without Dolby Tone).\r\n• The azimuth and gap-loss correction tools are the digital efforts of remedy in compensating minor imperfection of an analog tape player used for digitizing audio tapes.\r\n• The \"Play Trim\" is another digital tool for compensating weakened signal often found with a degraded pre-recorded tape.\r\n• The EQ Converter offers digital translation between 120μs and 70μs IEC tape equalization formulas — if such a flexibility is not found on a given tape player/recorder.\r\n• The built-in tone generator offers 400Hz 0dB signal at Dolby Reference Level for easy calibration.\r\n\r\nThese fine-tuning tools can work independently of the Dolby-B/C codec, which can also be applied for refining non-Dolby formatted audio. \r\n\r\nDDi Codec is a stand-alone GUI app without relying on any other DAW host.
